		<title>The World’s First Practice-Based Skill-Building App is Live</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/skill-building-app-cosmo/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/skill-building-app-cosmo/#respond</comments>

				<category><![CDATA[Features]]></category>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Get job-ready with Cosmo, CodeSignal’s new learning app with 300+ courses in AI, tech, business, finance, data, and other leading industries. </p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/skill-building-app-cosmo/">The World’s First Practice-Based Skill-Building App is Live</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-96902 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-app-banner.png" alt="Cosmo learning app banner – mobile tutor for GenAI, coding, marketing, finance, and leadership. Download on App Store or Google Play. Tagline: Turn screen time into skills time." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-app-banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-app-banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-app-banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>On LinkedIn, someone described the job market as “a market I never want to visit.” It is tough, brutal, even hostile.</p>
<p>If you’ve been hearing “we’ve decided to move forward with another candidate,” it doesn’t mean you’re not qualified — it usually means the competition had an edge in a few key areas.</p>
<ul>
<li>Their skills were more closely aligned with current employer needs.</li>
<li>They had more experience applying those skills in real-world settings.</li>
<li>They had AI capabilities that gave them an advantage.</li>
</ul>
<p>That’s where <a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a> comes in. <a href="https://codesignal.com?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">CodeSignal’s</a> new skill-building app helps you close these gaps by teaching you in-demand skills, giving you hands-on practice, and building your AI fluency so you can feel confident pursuing your next opportunity or promotion and stand out in the interview.</p>
<h2 id="turn-screen-time-into-hireable-skill-time">Turn Screen Time into (Hireable) Skill Time</h2>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a> is a free-to-download (on iOS, upcoming on Android on August 28), experiential learning web and mobile platform with 300+ bite-sized courses. You can build skills in accelerating fields like business, generative AI, tech, finance, coding, leadership, data, business, and personal growth.</p>
<p>The course catalog caters to the current industry demands. <a href="https://codesignal.com?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">CodeSignal</a>, a skill assessment and learning platform, has used its data from thousands of hiring companies to understand their needs and has built courses in response to their demand.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-96905 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard.png" alt="Two mobile app screens side by side. The first screen shows an online learning dashboard with categories such as GenAI, Marketing, Coding, Finance, and Growth, plus recommended courses like 'Generative AI for Business' and 'How to Start a Business.' The second screen displays an interactive coding lesson where a user is guided to write their first line of code using Python’s print function." width="1024" height="1027" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard-300x300.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard-1021x1024.png 1021w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard-150x150.png 150w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-dashboard-768x770.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>With a monthly or yearly subscription, you can access multiple courses and get shareable certifications that you can post on LinkedIn or attach to your resume.</p>
<p>Let’s see how you can <a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">use Cosmo</a> if you’re working in finance.</p>
<p>If you’re a finance professional looking to move into a higher-level role with more responsibility, leverage, and pay, the fastest way to stand out is to bridge the gap between finance and AI. Right now, leaders across the industry are <a href="https://hbr.org/2025/08/how-finance-teams-can-succeed-with-ai" target="_blank" rel="noopener">struggling to find talent</a> with both skill sets, and those who have them are in high demand.</p>
<p>On Cosmo, you can start with the GenAI in Finance course to build AI fluency in a finance context. Add Effective Leadership for Aspiring Managers to learn how to guide teams and drive change. Strengthen your analytical edge with Introduction to Data Analytics, so you can make better decisions with large, complex datasets.</p>
<p>Round it out with personal growth courses, and you’re not just a finance expert, you’re the forward-thinking leader companies are competing to hire.</p>
<p>These courses are bite-sized, but full of practice. Even if you’re a student or a recent graduate, you can accumulate skills by just spending a few minutes on Cosmo, not learning one way, but both ways.</p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p>“Cosmo makes learning hands-on from the very first tap. In five minutes, you might write a real GenAI prompt, fix a Python bug, tune an ad headline, or craft a follow-up email—small wins that stack into big career moves.”</p>
<p><em>— Tigran Sloyan, Co-Founder &amp; CEO, CodeSignal </em></p>
</div>
<h2 id="build-skills-that-get-you-hired">Build Skills That Get You Hired</h2>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a>, which is available to download on iOS and Android (from August 28), has 60+ learning paths (sequential content designed to reach a goal) across industries. Let’s take a current market favorite — AI.</p>
<h3>Cosmo’s Generative AI Courses</h3>
<p>Professionals with AI skills are <a href="https://www.pwc.com/gx/en/news-room/press-releases/2025/ai-linked-to-a-fourfold-increase-in-productivity-growth.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">earning more</a>, and the demand for employees with AI skills is higher.</p>
<p>Cosmo helps you become AI fluent — the ability to turn a task into a clear prompt, pick the right tool, and get output that matches your goal. You will learn the guardrails (privacy, bias, source checks) and use AI to get quick drafts, analysis, and for problem-solving.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-96904 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo.png" alt="Two mobile app screens side by side. The first screen shows an interactive quiz asking users to match GenAI capabilities such as generating code, writing blog posts, and creating marketing images with their best business use cases. The second screen displays a scenario card asking whether 'Marketing writer that matches brand voice perfectly' is better suited for a custom GPT use case or a regular AI tool." width="1024" height="1027" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo-300x300.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo-1021x1024.png 1021w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo-150x150.png 150w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-cosmo-768x770.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Cosmo makes sure you don’t just know AI, but you use it to streamline work and drive results. Anyone can take its Gen AI courses, since it’s the <a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/robinryan/2025/07/30/the-no-1-skill-employers-want-in-2025-and-most-job-seekers-dont-list-it/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">top skill</a> employers want.</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Beginners</b> who want to write clear prompts, summarize long docs, draft better emails, research, create slides, and double-check facts</li>
<li><b>Business and marketing professionals</b> who want to brainstorm creative concepts, draft campaigns, segment audiences, analyze spreadsheets, and turn notes into summaries</li>
<li><b>Technical professionals</b> in data, product, or engineering who want to write code, run SQL queries, fix bugs, and document and refactor code</li>
<li><b>Managers and team leads</b> who want to write job descriptions, draft performance feedback, and model scenarios with clear assumptions and citations</li>
<li><b>Advanced users </b>who want to build end-to-end solutions through prompt chaining, output refinement, multi-tool integration (docs, sheets, code), and automated quality assurance</li>
</ul>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p>&#8220;AI-empowered education&#8230; on steroids.&#8221;</p>
<p><em>&#8211; Cosmo Learner</em></p>
</div>
<p>Cosmo’s Gen AI courses are also spread across business, sales, marketing, HR, finance, engineering, analytics, healthcare, cybersecurity, project management, and product management. And if you’re a complete beginner or a student, you’ll find courses fit for you too.</p>
<h3>Advance in Your Job Role</h3>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a> offers targeted courses for different roles and career levels. Take leadership, for example. The courses cover three core competencies:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Understanding Humans</b></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>For People Managers</li>
<li>For Sales Managers</li>
<li>For Engineering Managers</li>
<li>For Aspiring Managers</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Effective Leadership</b></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>Principles</li>
<li>For Aspiring Managers</li>
<li>(Introduction) for Students</li>
<li>For Sales Leaders</li>
<li>For Engineering Leaders</li>
<li>For Recruiting Leaders</li>
<li>For Business Leaders</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Adaptive Leadership </b></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>Principles</li>
<li>For Sales Managers</li>
<li>For Business Leaders</li>
<li>For Engineering Managers</li>
<li>For Recruiting Leaders</li>
</ul>
<p>Beyond Gen AI and leadership, Cosmo provides hands-on courses in</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Finance</b> (economics, accounting, public markets, business valuations)</li>
<li><b>Marketing</b> (advertising, branding, demand generation, SEO, and content marketing)</li>
<li><b>Coding</b> (programming, JavaScript, Swift, Kotlin, Rust, web development, cloud computing)</li>
<li><b>Data</b> (SQL, data science (with Python), data analytics, machine learning, data engineering)</li>
<li><b>Business</b> (building a business, a tech startup, a local business, and influencer marketing)</li>
</ul>
<p>Plus, you’ll find <b>personal growth courses</b> to complement your professional journey. Cosmo has courses on building habits that stick, communicating confidently, decision-making, focusing, finding a career path, mastering personal finance, and critical thinking.</p>
<h2 id="why-does-cosmo-work">Why Does Cosmo Work?</h2>
<h3>Designed by CodeSignal</h3>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">CodeSignal</a>, with skills assessment and hands-on learning, helps organizations hire, train, and grow talent at scale while helping individuals advance their careers.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-96874 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-scaled.png" alt="CodeSignal AI-native skills assessment platform with verified scores, skill badges, and practice units to help organizations hire and train faster." width="2560" height="847" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-scaled.png 2560w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-300x99.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-1024x339.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-768x254.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-1536x508.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Screenshot-2025-08-15-at-2.48.05-AM-2048x677.png 2048w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2560px) 100vw, 2560px" /></p>
<p>It has offered millions of assessments to companies like Netflix, Capital One, Meta, and Dropbox and is used by learners worldwide to align their skills with evolving industries.</p>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a> is the result of these assessments, and the curriculum developers have studied data from 3000+ companies to spot the skills they need. Based on the gaps, they’ve designed courses and learning paths that make learning accessible and fun for everyone.</p>
<p>The strategy behind the learning experience is to cater to your mind. It tackles mental hurdles and learning challenges with solutions that work.</p>
<ul>
<li>Low attention span? Just spend minutes taking the courses, not long hours.</li>
<li>Struggling with concepts? Practice as you learn each skill.</li>
<li>Keep forgetting what you learned? Access the repetition feature to help knowledge stick.</li>
</ul>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p>“Fun, intuitive, and keeps you locked in.”</p>
<p><em>&#8211; Cosmo Learner</em></p>
</div>
<h3>Micro-Lessons Personalized for You</h3>
<p>The courses break a skill into tiny, focused reps you can do on your phone. Craft a specific AI prompt, write a Python snippet, or identify a good marketing hook — repeat similar tasks until you absorb the skill.</p>
<p>Each lesson is part of a learning path that will eventually lead to subject mastery and your certification.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-96903 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate.png" alt="Two mobile app screens side by side. The first screen shows a learning streak tracker with a 30-day streak, freeze protection, and a calendar view for August 2025. The second screen displays a certificate of achievement awarded to Nova Williams for completing the 'Front-End Engineering with React' learning path, with a button to share the certificate." width="1024" height="1027" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate-300x300.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate-1021x1024.png 1021w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate-150x150.png 150w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/codesignal-certificate-768x770.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Throughout every course, your AI tutor provides personalized hints and guidance for what to tackle next. Cosmo is designed around hands-on learning that fits your schedule. It’s built for your convenience and your pace.</p>
<p>“It’s like Duolingo, but for skills that actually get you a job.”</p>
<h2 id="the-big-question-what-does-it-cost">The Big Question — What Does it Cost?</h2>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cosmo</a> is free to download, and you can upgrade it for faster course progress. It uses the energy method to advance through the lessons. The free version of the mobile app is limited to 10 energy per day, which lets you complete a little over one unit per day.</p>
<p>The upgrade costs $24.99/month or $149.99/year in the US. This will get you access to your Cosmo+ subscription on your mobile and desktop.</p>
<h2 id="the-bottom-line-of-codesignal-s-cosmo">The Bottom Line of CodeSignal’s Cosmo App</h2>
<p>In a job market where a new skill becomes “a non-negotiable” within days, Cosmo is a reliable learning partner to stay relevant to employers. Built on years of CodeSignal&#8217;s assessment insights, it can offer you a strategic edge in the evolving job market.</p>
<p><a href="https://codesignal.com/learn-app/mobile?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Cosmo</a>, practice for just five minutes a day, and build the skills that can get you hired.</p>
<p><em>This article was produced by the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central Report</a> team in partnership with <a href="https://codesignal.com?utm_campaign=classcentral-courses_Q4_25_&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=classcentral&amp;utm_content=report" target="_blank" rel="noopener">CodeSignal</a>.</em></p>

		<title>[2025] 470+ Hours of Free LinkedIn Learning Courses with Free Certification</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/linkedin-learning-free-learning-paths/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/linkedin-learning-free-learning-paths/#comments</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Suparn Patra]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Thu, 21 Aug 2025 13:00:01 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Course Report]]></category>

		<category><![CDATA[LinkedIn Learning]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=72028</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>LinkedIn Learning is offering some free courses and learning paths including free certificates.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/linkedin-learning-free-learning-paths/">[2025] 470+ Hours of Free LinkedIn Learning Courses with Free Certification</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-77501 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/linked-learning-free-courses.png" alt="LinkedIn Learning Free Certificates" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/linked-learning-free-courses.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/linked-learning-free-courses-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/linked-learning-free-courses-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>LinkedIn Learning (previously Lynda.com) focuses on career skills. Most courses require a subscription, but in this <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a> article, we’ve compiled all the free LinkedIn Learning courses with certificates that we could find. These represent more than 470 hours of learning, including free certificates of completion.</p>
<h2><b>How it Started</b></h2>
<p>After the COVID-19 pandemic hit in 2020, Microsoft made <a href="https://blogs.microsoft.com/blog/2020/06/30/microsoft-launches-initiative-to-help-25-million-people-worldwide-acquire-the-digital-skills-needed-in-a-covid-19-economy/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14 learning paths on LinkedIn Learning</a> available for free. At the time, we shared the list of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/microcredentials/linkedin-learning-path" target="_blank" rel="noopener">learning paths</a> with free certificates, as well as a collection of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/free-online-learning-coronavirus/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free pandemic educational resources,</a> which was viewed by close to 1 million learners.</p>
<p>Since then, we’ve been keeping an eye on LinkedIn Learning, checking if there were more free LinkedIn Learning certificates available. I (Suparn) searched through their current catalog of over <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/linkedin-learning" target="_blank" rel="noopener">11,000 courses</a> and more than <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/microcredentials/linkedin-learning-path" target="_blank" rel="noopener">700 learning paths</a> and identified the courses available for free and that offer free certificates.</p>
<p>In 2022, I found 137 courses and 7 learning paths offering free certificates, as well as 378 free courses, for a total of about 1000 hours of free online learning. This was up from the initial 350 hours in 2020.</p>
<p>Since then, however, many of LinkedIn Learning’s courses are no longer free. But the good news is, there are still 115 free learning paths and 436 free courses in a range of languages.<br />
<!--Semrush bloc start--></p>
<div></div>
<h2><b>How to Join Free Certificate Courses</b></h2>
<p>When you join LinkedIn Learning, you are prompted to sign up for a 1-month free trial. To access the free courses, ignore the payment details screen after signing up (or signing in). Go back and select the course link in this article and you should now be able to go straight to the start of the course.</p>
<p>We’re not sure how long these courses will continue to offer free certificates. Courses seem to periodically swap from paid to free and back again.</p>
<p>If you find more free certificates or courses, or if you notice an error in the list, please tell us in the comments.</p>
<h2><b>More Free Certificates</b></h2>

<h2>How to earn a LinkedIn Learning Free Certificate</h2>
<figure id="attachment_74222" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-74222" style="width: 1756px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-74222 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup.png" alt="" width="1756" height="956" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup.png 1756w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup-300x163.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup-1024x557.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup-768x418.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Linkedin-Learning-Certificate-Popup-1536x836.png 1536w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1756px) 100vw, 1756px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-74222" class="wp-caption-text">LinkedIn Learning popup, to download your certificate</figcaption></figure>
<p>To earn a certificate for an individual course, watch all the videos and pass the quizzes. In some courses, you&#8217;ll need to take an exam. Once you&#8217;re done, go to the “Related to this course” section below the video (on desktop) and click on “Show all”.</p>
<p>A window will pop up with certificates available for the course, as you can see above. Click on “Download” to get your LinkedIn Learning certificate. Some courses also offer Continuing Professional Education (CPE) credits, in addition to the LinkedIn Learning certificate.</p>
<p>To earn a certificate for a learning path, you need to complete all the path&#8217;s courses. Then, you&#8217;ll be able to download the learning path certificate.</p>
<p>Here is the current list of free LinkedIn Learning Courses.</p>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Turn complex technical information into clear, concise, and reader-friendly documents with the help of these top technical writing courses.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-technical-writing-courses/">7 Best Technical Writing Courses to Master Documentation and Communication</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>

										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-96889" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-banner-color.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-banner-color.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-banner-color-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-banner-color-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>In 1999, NASA&#8217;s Mars Climate Orbiter spacecraft reached Mars after months of travel, but instead of entering orbit, it flew too close to the planet and burned up in the atmosphere. Why?</p>
<p>One team used feet and inches in the documents, while another used meters, and <a href="https://nssdc.gsfc.nasa.gov/nmc/spacecraft/display.action?id=1998-073A" target="_blank" rel="noopener">$327 million</a> and years of work were lost.</p>
<p>In 2016, another explosion happened — the Samsung Galaxy Note 7, which tended to explode due to the battery overheating. Despite urgent press releases, ads, and emails asking customers to return their devices, it took three months for most buyers to comply because the communication was <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/the-switch/wp/2016/09/15/consumer-product-safety-commission-issues-an-official-recall-for-the-galaxy-note-7/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">filled with confusing technical jargon</a> that masked the risks.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/technical-writing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Technical writing</a> isn&#8217;t just about making things simpler; it&#8217;s about building a standardized communication protocol that creates clear, concise, and accurate written materials for everyone.</p>
<p>It might seem easy to learn and master, but it demands an understanding of the audience and user experience, and attention to clarity and detail.</p>
<p>So I&#8217;ve curated the best technical writing courses from hundreds of options for aspiring writers and professionals who need to create technical documentation.</p>
<p>Head Directly to:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#why-learn-technical-writing">Why Learn Technical Writing?</a></li>
<li><a href="#why-trust-us-and-this-guide">Why Trust Us and This Guide?</a></li>
<li><a href="#best-technical-writing-courses">Best Technical Writing Courses</a></li>
<li><a href="#free-resources">Free Learning Resources</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="why-learn-technical-writing">Why Learn Technical Writing?</h2>
<p>Technical writing goes beyond avoiding confusion; it resolves the communication gap between those who create technology and those who use it.</p>
<p>For instance, <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/posts/bani-kaur-_quick-announcement-my-design-team-has-activity-7359296634301636608-TJX9?utm_source=share&amp;utm_medium=member_desktop&amp;rcm=ACoAACO2S_kBy9nbuNuN027LyAF5uO8LkuSgQYE" target="_blank" rel="noopener">a freelance technical writer</a> helped a B2B company build their annual salary report, which got 10,000 downloads! This helped their target audience get insights into the market, and it drove their website visits.</p>
<p>But technical writing is more than <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/report-writing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">reports</a> and manuals. Tech companies need <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/api-documentation" target="_blank" rel="noopener">clear API documentation</a>, hospitals need patient guides, and factories rely on safety instructions with no room for confusion.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-96908" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/types-of-technical-writing-fix.png" alt="" width="820" height="860" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/types-of-technical-writing-fix.png 820w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/types-of-technical-writing-fix-286x300.png 286w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/types-of-technical-writing-fix-768x805.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 820px) 100vw, 820px" /></p>
<p>You might’ve ordered a blood pressure machine and learned how to use it through its manual. Or if you’re a software developer, you might’ve relied on an API guide. Technical writing turns your anxiety and confusion into a clear, actionable state of mind. That isn’t easy.</p>
<p>Let’s look at <a href="https://careers.salesforce.com/en/jobs/jr307857/technical-writing-analyst/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">this Technical Writer job description</a>.</p>
<figure id="attachment_96846" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96846" style="width: 1558px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96846 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce.png" alt="" width="1558" height="714" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce.png 1558w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce-300x137.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce-1024x469.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce-768x352.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-salesforce-1536x704.png 1536w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1558px) 100vw, 1558px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96846" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://careers.salesforce.com/en/jobs/jr307857/technical-writing-analyst/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Source</a></figcaption></figure>
<p>Because it involves such intricate sub-skills, technical documentation is in demand (a freelance whitepaper writer can make anywhere between <a href="https://www.awai.com/inside-awai/writing-white-papers-1k-per-page/#:~:text=In%20our%20Copywriting%20Pricing%20Guide,project%20and%20your%20experience%20level." target="_blank" rel="noopener">$2,000 to $10,000</a> per project!).</p>
<p>While freelancers can take up multiple projects and charge well for them, employees can build leverage and solve problems with technical writing. A simple judgment of adding images to a manual, or clear onboarding guides that reduce training time by weeks, can create a massive difference. Good documentation saves time, prevents mistakes, and improves efficiency.</p>
<p>These courses equip you with the skills a technical writer needs, but before we get to them, let’s understand how I’ve handpicked them.</p>
<h2 id="why-trust-us-and-this-guide">Why Trust Us and This Guide?</h2>
<p>At <a href="https://www.classcentral.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a>, we’re building the &#8220;Tripadvisor for online education,&#8221; by helping you choose among <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">250,000 online courses</a>. We’ve helped over 100 million people find their next course. To make the choice quicker, we curate <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Courses Guides</a> that offer you the best free and paid resources to learn a skill.</p>
<p>For this guide, I took courses, watched interviews of technical writers, consulted with various technical writing firms, and studied multiple technical documents. This helped me choose courses that were high in quality and relevance.</p>
<p>When I started as an engineer, I spent months understanding the vocabulary, formatting, and language that go into technical documents. This is a list of courses I wish I had taken to write better technical documentation. There’s something in this list for everyone.</p>
<ul>
<li><b>For Beginners:</b> If you&#8217;re new to the technical writing field, start by understanding what it is. The first two courses help you understand technical writing, without overwhelming you. And your transition into it will be smoother with them.</li>
<li><b>For New and Aspiring Technical Writers:</b> If you want to become a valued technical writer, you’ll need to master audience needs, subject matter expert interviews, and clear, organized writing skills. The next three courses give you comprehensive knowledge and practical skills to develop your craft and market your writing.</li>
<li><b>For Professionals:</b> If you’re an engineer, manager, developer, or in another profession, you might be spending hours writing and building technical content. If you want to feel confident while writing, the last two resources will help you with that.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="best-for-beginners-udemy"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-introduction-to-technical-writing-403075" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best for Beginners (Udemy)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Beginner</li>
<li><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 ★ (2,000+ ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration:</b> 2-3 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid (varies)</li>
<li><b>Assignments</b>: No</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96850" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96850" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-introduction-to-technical-writing-403075" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96850 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-beginner-udemy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-beginner-udemy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-beginner-udemy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-beginner-udemy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96850" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Udemy</figcaption></figure>
<p>The first time I had to create product documentation, I felt completely lost. I was confident in my writing, but not in structuring technical information.</p>
<p>If you’re in a similar spot, whether you&#8217;re a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-product-management-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">product manager</a>, engineer, or <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-creative-writing-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">writer</a>, then <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-introduction-to-technical-writing-403075" target="_blank" rel="noopener">this course, by Dr. Katharina Grimm</a>, will reduce that initial anxiety.</p>
<p>It walks you through what technical writing is (and isn’t), and how to plan, draft, and polish professional documentation from scratch.</p>
<p>The modules cover the basics like structuring documents, ensuring quality, editing for clarity, and diving into the planning strategies and metadata, which are often skipped in beginner courses.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>This course provides a detailed, structured, and foundational understanding of crafting clear and concise technical documents.</li>
<li>It gives beginners rules to follow, helping them feel more confident in producing their documentation.</li>
<li>The instructor&#8217;s brief yet informative style was engaging without being overwhelming.</li>
<li>Learners reported a boost in confidence, noting that the course encouraged them to dive deeper into technical writing.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<ul>
<li>The course doesn’t go deep into advanced concepts, so it’s better suited for beginners only.</li>
<li>The course also lacks guided assignments, which can help practice technical writing skills.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>Engineers, product managers, or writers who have recently started working on documentation and are looking for a simple, quick, and beginner-friendly course.</p>
<h2 id="best-master-class-udemy"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-tech-writers-master-class-105375" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Master Class (Udemy)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Beginner</li>
<li><b>Rating:</b> 4.3★ (2,000+ ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration:</b> 6 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid (varies)</li>
<li><b>Assignments</b>: Yes</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96853" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96853" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-tech-writers-master-class-105375" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96853 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-masterclass-udemy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-masterclass-udemy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-masterclass-udemy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-masterclass-udemy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96853" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Udemy</figcaption></figure>
<p>If you&#8217;re just getting started with technical writing and need guidance to draft your first document, check this one out.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-tech-writers-master-class-105375" target="_blank" rel="noopener">This Master Class by Janet Underwood</a> keeps things simple, focused, and practical. It&#8217;s designed for beginners who want to test the waters of technical writing without heavy theory or overproduction.</p>
<p>The course walks you through everything from word choice and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-english-grammar-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">sentence structure</a> to formatting, document types, and even usability testing (watching real users try a product to find what&#8217;s confusing or hard to use).</p>
<p>What stood out is how easy this course is to follow. You won’t be buried in jargon, and the pace is perfect for beginners or career changers on a budget.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>What stood out most was the clear and simplified teaching style that welcomes absolute beginners without overwhelming them.</li>
<li>The instructor explains core writing principles, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/document-formatting" target="_blank" rel="noopener">document formatting</a>, and graphics usage in a practical, approachable way.</li>
<li>The lessons are short, well-organized, and easy to navigate, making it simple to absorb the material even if you’re learning in short breaks.</li>
<li>Learners have praised the straightforward structure, real examples, and useful templates. Some have also mentioned how the course has helped them apply skills immediately, without complication.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<p>It lacks depth for intermediate or advanced learners, but it&#8217;s a solid launchpad for exploring the field.</p>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>Tech professionals or writers looking to transition into technical writing.</p>
<h2 id="great-for-aspiring-technical-writers-udemy"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-101-for-beginners-476173" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Great for Aspiring Technical Writers (Udemy)</a></h2>
<ul>

<li><b>Duration:</b> 2 Hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid (varies)</li>
<li><b>Assignments</b>: Yes</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96848" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96848" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-101-for-beginners-476173" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96848 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-aspiring-udemy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-aspiring-udemy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-aspiring-udemy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-aspiring-udemy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96848" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Udemy</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-for-everyone-476174" target="_blank" rel="noopener">This course</a> is a great entry point for anyone curious about technical writing. It’s taught by Leigh Hartzman, a content and localization strategist at Google, who has designed the curriculum to teach you to create clear, concise, and customer-centric instructions for a variety of products.</p>
<p>The course is highly practical, walking you through writing common types of instructions, such as FAQs, how-to articles, and troubleshooting.</p>
<p>You&#8217;ll get hands-on experience by completing assignments in a fictional scenario, which allows you to apply what you&#8217;ve learned to a real-world context. The course also includes valuable lessons on working with product managers and other team members.</p>
<h2 id="why-i-picked-this-course">Why I Picked This Course:</h2>
<ul>
<li>It is taught by Leigh Hartzman, who has worked as a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/content-strategy" target="_blank" rel="noopener">content strategist</a> at Google and Waze. So, you’re learning from the master of clarity and precision.</li>
<li>The course focuses on instructional writing that’s clear, concise, and accessible to diverse audiences.</li>
<li>Complex concepts are broken into short, focused lessons like writing FAQs, step sequences, and troubleshooters. It makes learning digestible and immediately applicable.</li>
<li>Each topic is accompanied by fun quizzes and real-world assignments.</li>
<li>The course consists of real-world scenarios. You play the role of a technical writer in scenarios involving product managers and support teams to craft knowledge base articles and troubleshooting guides.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="cons">Cons:</h2>
<ul>
<li>Some learners felt the material was too basic for technical writers who want to advance in their careers.</li>
<li>The slide design could be more engaging and sophisticated.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="best-for">Best for:</h2>
<p>Those who want to explore technical writing as a career by creating diverse documents (articles, manuals, instructions).</p>
<h2 id="best-for-new-technical-writers-udemy"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-and-editing-86380" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best for New Technical Writers (Udemy)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Intermediate</li>
<li><b>Rating:</b> 4.5★ (800+ ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration: </b>16 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> $15–$20 (not included in Udemy Subscription)</li>
<li><b>Assignment:</b> Yes</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96854" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96854" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-and-editing-86380" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96854 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-new-udemy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-new-udemy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-new-udemy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-new-udemy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96854" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Udemy</figcaption></figure>
<p>When I say this course felt like the holy grail of technical writing, I’m not exaggerating. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-and-editing-86380" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Dr. Ugur Akinci’s Professional Technical Writing</a> is one of the most comprehensive and practice-focused courses.</p>
<p>Despite the higher price point (and it’s not part of Udemy’s subscription plan), this course justifies every cent. It combines professional-level guidance with a hands-on approach: you’ll build a real portfolio project, create your first user guide, and even get feedback from the instructor.</p>
<p>From document structure and clarity to editing and formatting, the course covers it all with downloadable templates and assignments that mimic real-world tasks.</p>
<p>Dr. Akinci is highly responsive, offering guidance that feels more like mentorship than passive instruction. Many learners have used this course to transition into technical writing roles, enhance their professional portfolios, or sharpen <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-business-english-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">workplace communication</a> skills.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>I chose this course because it combines a clear, methodical teaching style with decades of real-world experience from a Fortune 100 technical writer.</li>
<li>His structured lessons cover everything that one needs, from <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/grammar-writing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">grammar and writing</a> principles to document design and industry tools.</li>
<li>What stood out to me was the hands-on approach: practical exercises and a final project with personalized feedback</li>
<li>It can be used by both aspiring technical writers and STEM professionals to learn all about technical writing.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<p>The course was last updated in 2019. Some parts might seem outdated, but it teaches core technical writing skills well.</p>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>Both STEM professionals exploring technical writing and new writers who want strong foundational skills and a portfolio as technical writers.</p>
<h2 id="career-launcher-for-aspiring-technical-writers-udemy"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-for-everyone-476174" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Career Launcher for Technical Writers (Udemy)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Beginner</li>
<li><b>Rating:</b> 4.5★ (200+ ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration:</b> 1.5 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid</li>
<li><b>Assignment:</b> Yes</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96852" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96852" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-for-everyone-476174" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96852 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-launcher-udemy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-launcher-udemy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-launcher-udemy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-launcher-udemy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96852" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Udemy</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-technical-writing-for-everyone-476174" target="_blank" rel="noopener">This course</a>, created by Growth School, is designed for anyone new to technical writing. It&#8217;s a beginner-friendly guide that aims to help you master the skills needed to create clear, concise, and impactful technical documents.</p>
<p>The curriculum is practical, covering everything from the fundamental principles of technical writing to the use of various tools and software. It is structured to help you understand how to create a technical document from scratch, how to structure it for maximum efficiency, and how to write in a user-friendly way.</p>
<p>A key focus of this course is not just learning the theory, but also building a professional portfolio, which is essential for landing a job.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>It offers comprehensive content for beginners.</li>
<li>Has a strong emphasis on practical skills and real-world applications.</li>
<li>It is suitable for a wide range of professionals, including writers, engineers, and project managers.</li>
<li>The content is designed to help you get a competitive edge in the job market.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<ul>
<li>The course assignments are marked by users. No evaluation by the instructor.</li>
<li>The instructor has a heavy accent, but switching on the subtitles helps.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>New technical writers or career changers who want a structured course with the goal of landing their first technical writing job/gig.</p>
<h2 id="best-for-documentation-writing-coursera"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/technical-writing-introduction-263696" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best for Documentation Writing (Coursera)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Beginner</li>
<li><b>Rating: </b>4.6 ★ (350+ ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration:</b> ~15 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid (free preview)</li>
<li><b>Assignments: </b>Yes</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96851" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96851" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/technical-writing-introduction-263696" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96851 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-documentation.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-documentation.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-documentation-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg-technical-writing-documentation-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96851" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Coursera</figcaption></figure>
<p>If you’re looking to grasp technical writing concepts quickly but still want a structured approach that takes you through the process, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/technical-writing-introduction-263696" target="_blank" rel="noopener">take this course.</a></p>
<p>It guides you from the history and fundamentals of technical writing to <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-user-experience-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">design principles</a>, document types, and ethical practices.</p>
<p>This one can be a go-to for interns, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/data-analysis" target="_blank" rel="noopener">analysts</a>, junior managers, engineers, and IT professionals who are suddenly asked to create documentation and don’t know where to begin.</p>
<p>The modular design means you can start with the basics and build toward advanced skills, such as creating API documentation, ensuring accessibility, and even writing for emerging tech like VR and AR.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>It has step-by-step lessons on planning, structuring, and polishing documents.</li>
<li>It focuses on visual design like <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/typography" target="_blank" rel="noopener">typography</a>, layout, and navigation aids.</li>
<li>The course has ethical considerations, localization strategies, and inclusive communication.</li>
<li>Student reviews often highlight the clear, easy-to-follow videos, helpful transcripts for clarity, and a steady pace that works well for non-native English speakers.</li>
<li>While some learners wanted more project-based assignments or deeper dives into specialized topics like SEO and API documentation, most found the course engaging, comprehensive, and confidence-boosting.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<p>The audio track is slightly muffled, so switching on the captions would help.</p>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>Professionals who are asked to write documentation or reports and want a quick introduction to technical writing.</p>
<h2 id="best-for-software-documentation-writing-pluralsight"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-technical-writing-software-documentation-476175" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best for Software Documentation Writing (Pluralsight)</a></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Level:</b> Beginner</li>
<li><b>Rating: </b>4.5 ★ (300 ratings)</li>
<li><b>Duration:</b> ~4 hours</li>
<li><b>Cost:</b> Paid (subscription)</li>
<li><b>Assignments:</b> No</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_96847" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96847" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-technical-writing-software-documentation-476175" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96847 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg_cobol_pluralsight_tom_murach_mainframe.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg_cobol_pluralsight_tom_murach_mainframe.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg_cobol_pluralsight_tom_murach_mainframe-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bcg_cobol_pluralsight_tom_murach_mainframe-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96847" class="wp-caption-text">Source: Pluralsight</figcaption></figure>
<p>An efficient developer might not always be an efficient communicator. If you struggle to build documents that your teams can refer to, then <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-technical-writing-software-documentation-476175" target="_blank" rel="noopener">this course is for you</a>.</p>
<p>It teaches you to write five kinds of documents: requirements, architecture/design docs, code documentation, test plans, and user manuals.</p>
<p>Even if you’re a new developer, you can take this course because it starts by defining technical writing and then moves on to best practices, design, and more.</p>
<h3>Why I Picked This Course:</h3>
<ul>
<li>It’s a short overview, but it touches every software documentation essential, enough for you to approach technical writing confidently.</li>
<li>The instructor, Amber Israelsen, is a developer, author, and technical trainer, so she simplifies writing terms and advice.</li>
<li>It covers grammar, tone, and structure, making it helpful for employees who aren’t fluent in written English.</li>
<li>The instructor maps out the writing process and includes stories to help students learn better.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Cons:</h3>
<p>The course doesn’t offer practical training. It’s more instructional than experiential.</p>
<h3>Best for:</h3>
<p>New developers, engineers, and project managers who need to create professional software documentation but struggle with clarity, tone, and structure.</p>
<p><b>P.S.</b> If you’re looking for an advanced API writing course, you can go through <a href="https://idratherbewriting.com/learnapidoc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tom Johnson’s free Documenting APIs course</a> (mentioned below).</p>
<h2 id="free-resources">Free Resources</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://developers.google.com/tech-writing" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Technical Writing Resource (Google)</b></a> is a free and self-paced technical writing course by Google for engineers, developers, and tech professionals. It covers clarity, structure, and readability with short guides and exercises. It is ideal for improving documentation skills, especially for non-native English speakers.</li>
<li><a href="https://www.writethedocs.org/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Write the Docs</b></a> stands out as a vibrant, community-driven resource with several collaborative guides, templates, and talks for both new and experienced documentarians. It is great for software developers.</li>
<li><a href="https://alison.com/course/technical-writing-essentials" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Alison’s Technical Writing Essentials</b></a> is great for beginners because it provides a comprehensive, free-to-audit fundamentals course that covers all the basics of technical communication.</li>
<li><a href="https://roadmap.sh/technical-writer" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Roadmap.sh/technical-writer</b></a> offers a visually oriented and structured learning path for those who want to understand how to apply technical writing skills to the rapidly evolving field of AI.</li>
<li><a href="https://youtu.be/qzLPwc5Xjkc?si=75s-FdWaLQuSfX_S" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Henry Harvin’s YouTube Playlist</b></a> provides a series of free, accessible videos that break down the core concepts of technical writing for beginners.</li>
<li><a href="https://idratherbewriting.com/learnapidoc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><b>Tom Johnson’s ‘Documenting APIs’ Course</b></a> is a <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/technicalwriting/comments/12tk0k6/api_documentation/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Reddit favorite</a> and the gold standard for learning API documentation. It includes practical exercises and detailed learning on the documentation process.</li>
</ul>
<p>Now that you&#8217;ve explored the best technical writing courses, the next step is to choose the one that aligns with your goals. With these courses, you’ll find the right training in technical communication. You can master the art of clear communication, prevent costly mistakes, and add an invaluable skill to your professional toolkit.</p>

		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Dhawal Shah]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Wed, 20 Aug 2025 13:00:48 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Course Report]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Coursera]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=66895</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Did you know Coursera has some courses that are still completely free? Class Central has the complete list.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-free-online-courses/">[2025] 300+ Coursera Courses Still Completely Free</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-74380 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/coursera-free-courses.png" alt="Free courses on Coursera" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/coursera-free-courses.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/coursera-free-courses-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/coursera-free-courses-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Is Coursera Free?</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">At </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Class Central</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, we get that question so often that I wrote </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">a guide to answer it</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Coursera’s entire catalog used to be entirely free. But in late 2015, they </span><a href="https://blog.coursera.org/an-update-on-assessments-grades-and/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">introduced a paywall</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. Over the following years, this monetization approach expanded to other online course providers, </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/edx-paywall-graded-assignments/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">including edX</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. </span>Most Coursera courses were free to audit, but if you wanted to complete graded assignments or get a course certificate, you had to pay.</p>
<p>In mid-2025, Coursera introduced <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-preview-mode-paywall/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Preview Mode</a>, which allows full access to the first module of courses, including the graded items. To progress further, though, you need to pay.</p>
<figure id="attachment_96802" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96802" style="width: 2482px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-96802" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate.png" alt="" width="2482" height="1359" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate.png 2482w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate-300x164.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate-1024x561.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate-768x421.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate-1536x841.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08FullCourseNoCertificate-2048x1121.png 2048w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2482px) 100vw, 2482px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96802" class="wp-caption-text">Free Coursera course: “Full Course, No Certificate” (with graded assignments)</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">But I wondered if there were a few courses on Coursera that remained completely free. When you enroll in these courses, they offer a “</span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Full Course, No Certificate</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;">” option, as you can see above.</span></p>
<p><!--Semrush bloc start-->The more restrictive free-to-audit option, which doesn’t include graded assignments, appears to have been withdrawn. Many courses now have a Preview option, that allows you to access the first module of the course (including graded items) without entering payment details such as a credit card. This option is quite easy to miss. You have to look for the “<i>Preview</i>” link at the very bottom of the window that pops up when you enroll.</p>
<figure id="attachment_96803" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96803" style="width: 2482px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-96803" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure.png" alt="" width="2482" height="1359" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure.png 2482w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure-300x164.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure-1024x561.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure-768x421.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure-1536x841.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/2025-08PreviewForFreeGoogleCloudFundamentalsCoreInfrastructure-2048x1121.png 2048w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2482px) 100vw, 2482px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96803" class="wp-caption-text">Free Preview option</figcaption></figure>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Which Courses are Entirely Free?</span></h2>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large">
<p><i>With the phasing-out of free audit mode, I feared that no courses would remain completely free. But out of Coursera’s 15,000+ active courses, we found more than 300 fully free courses.</i></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The biggest challenge is finding </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">which</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Coursera courses are entirely free. The Coursera website doesn’t provide any “free course” filter (</span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/coursera?free=true" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Class Central does though</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> ). To know if a course is fully free, you have to log into Coursera, enroll in the course, and look for the “</span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Full Course, No Certificate</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;">” option.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">But there are thousands of courses on Coursera, so short of checking them one by one, it’s tricky to manually put together a list of their fully-free courses. So instead, we went with an automated approach.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Originally, I used the browser automation tool </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/selenium" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Selenium</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> to check the courses for me. My colleague </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@bob" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Bob</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> set me up with an </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/aws" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">AWS instance</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and </span><a href="https://aws.amazon.com/cloud9/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Cloud9 IDE</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, where I could do this automation. Below is a screenshot of the setup. (Yes, I prefer PHP.)</span></p>
<figure id="attachment_85415" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85415" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-85415" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php.png" alt="" width="1536" height="950" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php-300x186.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php-1024x633.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cloud9-selenium-php-768x475.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85415" class="wp-caption-text">Automating the search for free Coursera courses with Selenium</figcaption></figure>
<p>With the phasing-out of free audit mode, I feared that no courses would remain completely free. But out of Coursera’s 15,000+ active courses, we found more than 300 fully free courses (that is, including the graded assignments, minus only the free certificate).</p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free Coursera Courses</span></h2>

		<item>
		<title>2025&#8217;s Online Education Shakeup Claims Another: Skillshare&#8217;s CEO Departs</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/skillshare-new-ceo-paul-slavin/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/skillshare-new-ceo-paul-slavin/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Dhawal Shah]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Tue, 19 Aug 2025 18:35:15 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[News]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=96817</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Matt Cooper exits after nine years as the creative learning platform shows signs of struggle, from outdated press pages to courses appearing on rival Coursera.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/skillshare-new-ceo-paul-slavin/">2025&#8217;s Online Education Shakeup Claims Another: Skillshare&#8217;s CEO Departs</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-96828" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-new-ceo-2025.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-new-ceo-2025.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-new-ceo-2025-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-new-ceo-2025-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>2025 is proving to be a tough year for CEOs at online education companies. Following changes at <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-ceo-jeff-maggioncalda-retires/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Coursera</a> and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-mckinsey-ceo-as-growth-struggles/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Udemy</a>, it’s now Skillshare’s turn to appoint a new CEO.</p>
<p>I learned about this when Matt Cooper <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/posts/cooperm_big-career-news-after-almost-9-incredible-activity-7363559114272104448-ftJK/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">announced his departure on LinkedIn</a>. He had been with the company for almost nine years, serving first as COO before becoming CEO. Although Skillshare <a href="https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20250811766802/en/Skillshare-Names-Paul-Slavin-as-Chief-Executive-Officer" target="_blank" rel="noopener">published a press release</a>, its official channels have been quiet, and its <a href="https://www.skillshare.com/en/press" target="_blank" rel="noopener">press page</a> hasn’t been updated since July 2023, a small telling signal that something isn&#8217;t right.</p>
<p>Think of Skillshare as Udemy&#8217;s creative cousin, offering courses that focus on hands-on projects in areas like design, photography, animation, and video. It operates on a subscription-only model, which costs $168 per year in the United States.</p>
<figure id="attachment_96821" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96821" style="width: 2560px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-96821" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-scaled.png" alt="Skillshare pricing page showing subscription cost of $13.99 per month billed annually at $167.88, with sign-up option." width="2560" height="880" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-scaled.png 2560w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-300x103.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-1024x352.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-768x264.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-1536x528.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-pricing-page-2025-2048x704.png 2048w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 2560px) 100vw, 2560px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96821" class="wp-caption-text">Skillshare charges $167.88 annually for its subscription, or $13.99 per month billed yearly</figcaption></figure>
<p>Skillshare’s new CEO, Paul Slavin, is a former senior executive at ABC News. The <a href="https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20250811766802/en/Skillshare-Names-Paul-Slavin-as-Chief-Executive-Officer" target="_blank" rel="noopener">press release</a> provides more details about his background.</p>
<p>In recent months, I noticed another potential sign of trouble: some Skillshare courses started appearing on Coursera. When a platform lists its courses with a larger competitor, it’s a clear indication that it is likely struggling for revenue and is willing to sacrifice brand exclusivity for greater reach.</p>
<figure id="attachment_96819" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-96819" style="width: 1200px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96819 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-1-on-1-sessions-screen-2025.jpg" alt="Screenshot of Skillshare 1-on-1 Sessions page showing instructor profiles with names, photos, expertise, and session prices across categories like art, design, writing, and music." width="1200" height="651" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-1-on-1-sessions-screen-2025.jpg 1200w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-1-on-1-sessions-screen-2025-300x163.jpg 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-1-on-1-sessions-screen-2025-1024x556.jpg 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/skillshare-1-on-1-sessions-screen-2025-768x417.jpg 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-96819" class="wp-caption-text">Skillshare’s 1-on-1 Sessions, launched after its Superpeer acquisition.</figcaption></figure>
<p>Skillshare&#8217;s last major strategic play was its acquisition of Superpeer last year. This move has allowed the company to expand its offerings beyond online classes to include <a href="https://www.skillshare.com/en/one-on-one-sessions" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1-on-1 coaching</a> and a <a href="https://www.skillshare.com/en/shop/digital-products" target="_blank" rel="noopener">shop for digital products</a> including brushes, ebooks, guides, and workbooks. The company has also been <a href="https://www.youtube.com/@Skillshare/streams" target="_blank" rel="noopener">livestreaming on YouTube</a>, though viewership for these videos is typically in the low hundreds.</p>
<p>As far as I can tell, none of these have produced results that would satisfy a VC-backed company, so as Matt Cooper said in his LinkedIn note, &#8220;It&#8217;s time for new leadership, fresh ideas, and the next chapter.&#8221;</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/skillshare-new-ceo-paul-slavin/">2025&#8217;s Online Education Shakeup Claims Another: Skillshare&#8217;s CEO Departs</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></content:encoded>
					
					<wfw:commentRss>https://www.classcentral.com/report/skillshare-new-ceo-paul-slavin/feed/</wfw:commentRss>
