		<item>
		<title>[2025] 100 Top FREE Coursera Courses of All Time</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-top-courses/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-top-courses/#comments</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Suparn Patra]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Tue, 19 Aug 2025 11:50:40 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Course Report]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Coursera]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=76388</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>A list of Coursera’s 100 most popular free online courses. Combined, they’ve gathered over 7M enrollments.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-top-courses/">[2025] 100 Top FREE Coursera Courses of All Time</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-76386" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/coursera-top-courses.png" alt="Top Free Courses of All Time" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/coursera-top-courses.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/coursera-top-courses-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/coursera-top-courses-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://coursera.pxf.io/c/259799/1242836/14726?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.coursera.org%2F&amp;subId1=" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Coursera</a>, founded in the heyday of the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-hype-year-1/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">MOOC hype</a>, is one of the world’s largest <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-providers-list/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online course providers</a> and boasts an active catalog of over 15,000 courses, up from 12,000+ last year.</p>
<p>Boosted by the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/the-second-year-of-the-mooc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">momentum provided by the COVID-19 pandemic</a> to online education companies, Coursera went public in March, 2021. Class Central’s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-s1-analysis/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">analysis of Coursera’s IPO</a> filing showed that the company made $293.5M revenue in 2020. In 2021, the company<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-q4-2021/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> made $415.3M</a>. To learn more about Coursera, read our analysis of their business: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-economics/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">A Deep Dive Into Coursera’s Financials</a>.</p>
<p>In 2022, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-q2-2022/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Coursera&#8217;s stock dropped by 20%</a> due to a degree enrollments slowdown in the US as well as headwinds for their consumer and business segments in Europe.</p>
<p>Coursera experienced <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-q4-2023/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">strong growth in 2023</a>, adding 24 million new learners and increasing revenue by 21% to $636 million, driven primarily by its consumer business and tech partnerships. However, the company <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-annual-report-2023/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">faced challenges in early 2024</a>, revising down its revenue projections and experiencing a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-q1-2024/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">significant stock price drop</a>, while focusing on expanding its AI-related offerings and proprietary content to drive future growth.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-96617 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/coursera-segment-growth-q2-2025.png" alt="Line chart titled &quot;Coursera: Segment Growth&quot; showing rising revenue from consumer, enterprise, and total segments from 2020 to Q2 2025. Total revenue reached $187.1M in Q2 2025." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/coursera-segment-growth-q2-2025.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/coursera-segment-growth-q2-2025-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/coursera-segment-growth-q2-2025-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>At one time, Coursera’s courses were completely free. But as time went on and Coursera <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-monetization-revenues/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">focused on monetization</a>, graded assignments and certificates were put behind a paywall. Eventually the courses went from free to “free to audit”. In mid-2025, Coursera introduced <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-preview-mode-paywall/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Preview Mode</a>, all but eliminating free to audit mode and drastically reducing the number of completely free courses.</p>
<p>But an investigation by Class Central found that there are still <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-free-online-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">300 completely free courses on Coursera</a> (minus the certificate). If you have trouble signing up for audit or preview mode, please read our guide on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">How to Sign up for Coursera Courses for Free</a>.</p>
<h2>100 Most Popular FREE Coursera Courses</h2>
<p>Here’s a quick summary of Coursera’s 100 most popular free online courses of all time, based on the number of enrollments:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Enrollments range from <b>6K</b> to <b>1.4M</b>. Only one course has over <b>1M</b> enrollments</li>
<li aria-level="1">Together, they account for over <b>7M</b> enrollments, with an average of <b>71K</b> per course</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>88</b> courses are in English; the rest are in various other languages</li>
<li aria-level="1">They’ve received <b>726</b> reviews on Class Central, averaging <b>12 </b>reviews each</li>
<li aria-level="1">Average rating: <b>4.57/5.0</b></li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>35</b> courses are beginner level, <b>15</b> are intermediate level, and <b>2</b> are advanced level. The rest are mixed levels.</li>
<li aria-level="1">In total, the courses offer <b>1,500+</b> hours of learning.</li>
</ul>
<p>Here are the courses:</p>
<ol>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/algs4partI-339" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Algorithms, Part I</a> from <em>Princeton University</em> ★★★★☆(62)</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/bitcointech-3655" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Bitcoin and Cryptocurrency Technologies</a> from <em>Princeton University</em> ★★★★★(19)</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs-programming-java-13151" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computer Science: Programming with a Purpose</a> from <em>Princeton University</em> ★★★★★(1)</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/lesson-small-talk-and-conversational-vocabulary-17922" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Lesson | Small Talk &amp; Conversational Vocabulary</a> from <em>Georgia Institute of Technology</em> ★★★★★(1)</li>

		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=88613</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Including thousands of free certificates and badges from these leading big tech companies.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/big-tech-free-courses/">10,000+ Free Courses from Tech Giants: Learn from Google, Microsoft, Amazon, and More</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92621 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/big-tech-free-courses-banner-10k-update.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/big-tech-free-courses-banner-10k-update.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/big-tech-free-courses-banner-10k-update-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/big-tech-free-courses-banner-10k-update-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Did you know that big tech companies — such as Google, Microsoft, and Amazon — offer thousands of free online courses? Many of them even include free certificates and badges.</p>
<p>These tech giants offer courses mainly to teach people about their products and associated technologies. Since these companies are so expansive, we end up with courses for both beginners and power users, covering many subjects: programming, data science, cloud technology, business… you name it.</p>
<p>The challenge is finding all these courses, since they tend to live on separate platforms. So <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a> did the legwork for you: we compiled them all in this article, testing the platforms as needed, and collecting a few certificates along the way, which you can find below.</p>
<p>We’ll continue to update this article in the future. If you know another relevant platform that isn’t included here yet, please let us know in the comments, and we’ll add it to the article.</p>
<p><b>Please note</b>, Class Central is not involved in running the courses or issuing certificates. This is a dynamic field and you may discover that a course you choose is no longer available or free, or doesn’t have a free certificate any more. We recommend you always check before starting a course.</p>
<div></div>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Table of Contents</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Click on a company to jump to their free courses and certificates.</span></p>
<div class="table">
<table class="fancy-table">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><a href="#google"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google</span></a></td>
<td><b>450</b><strong>+</strong><span style="font-weight: 400;"> free certificates and badges on Android, cloud, analytics, digital marketing&#8230;</span></td>
</tr>

<figure id="attachment_88623" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88623" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/microsoft.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-88623 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/microsoft.png" alt="" width="1024" height="630" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/microsoft.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/microsoft-300x185.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/microsoft-768x473.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88623" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/author/manoel/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Manoel&#8217;s</a> free <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/microsoft-learn-develop-natural-language-processing-solutions-with-azure-ai-services-262538" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Microsoft NLP with Azure free certificate</a></figcaption></figure>
<p>Microsoft is another big tech generalist, known for Windows, the Office software suite, its Azure cloud computing platform, and in the gaming industry with Xbox, among others. To support and expand the skills related to these and other technologies, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/microsoft" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Microsoft offers over 3,000 online courses</a> with 2,800+ currently free.</p>
<p>Microsoft’s courses are primarily available through <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/microsoft-learn" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Microsoft Learn</a>, an interactive, hands-on platform that offers free access to learning paths and modules. Besides, they provide additional courses via Coursera and edX, most free-to-audit. Finally, they offer courses on <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/linkedin-learning-free-learning-paths/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">LinkedIn Learning</a>, which they acquired.</p>
<p>Learning paths on Microsoft Learn include free badges. By contrast, their certifications typically require payment. In 2023, Microsoft launched a new type of credential, <a href="https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/microsoft-learn-blog/announcing-microsoft-applied-skills-the-new-credentials-to/ba-p/3775645" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Applied Skills</a>, and these are free for a limited time. Upon completion of an Applied Skill assessment, you’ll receive a free certificate.</p>

<h2 id="aws"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free Amazon (AWS) Courses &amp; Certificates</span></h2>
<figure id="attachment_88624" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88624" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/aws.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-88624 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/aws.png" alt="" width="1024" height="757" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/aws.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/aws-300x222.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/aws-768x568.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88624" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/author/manoel/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Manoel&#8217;s</a> free AWS Intro to AI certificate (no longer available)</figcaption></figure>
<p>Amazon Web Services (AWS) is the cloud computing arm of the global e-commerce leader, Amazon. To educate users in their cloud technology, AWS offers a substantial number of online courses.</p>
<p>Among the over <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/amazon" target="_blank" rel="noopener">9,000 Amazon courses</a>, more than 720 are courses, learning paths, and game-based courses with free certificates or badges specifically from AWS. These programs are designed to help learners grasp the fundamentals of AWS services and advance towards more complex applications.</p>
<p>AWS’ free courses can be accessed via:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/aws-skill-builder" target="_blank" rel="noopener">AWS Skill Builder</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://aws.amazon.com/education/awseducate/?nc2=sb_ep_edu" target="_blank" rel="noopener">AWS Educate</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Besides providing extensive resources on cloud computing, the platforms cover broader subjects, such as cybersecurity, data science, generative AI, and algorithms.</p>
<p>Here’s are some popular offerings:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-of-prompt-engineering-264566" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Foundations of Prompt Engineering</i></a><i> from Amazon Web Services ★★★★★(2)</i></li>

Around 60 courses offer a completion badge or certificate. Check on the <a href="https://cognitiveclass.ai/badges" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cognitive Class.AI</a> course page for details.</p>

<h2 id="linkedin"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free LinkedIn Learning Courses &amp; Certificates</span></h2>
<figure id="attachment_88626" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88626" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/linkedin.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-88626 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/linkedin.png" alt="" width="1024" height="822" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/linkedin.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/linkedin-300x241.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/linkedin-768x617.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88626" class="wp-caption-text">My colleague <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/author/suparn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@suparn</a>&#8216;s free LinkedIn Customer Service Foundations certificate (not currently free)</figcaption></figure>
<p>LinkedIn Learning, an extension of the professional networking site LinkedIn owned by Microsoft, offers over <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/linkedin-learning" target="_blank" rel="noopener">14,000 online courses</a> designed to enhance skills across various domains. Among these, some courses are not only free but also include the benefit of earning a certificate upon completion.</p>
<p>The platform covers a wide range of topics, from business and technology to creative fields. The courses are designed to be practical and applicable, helping professionals stay current with industry trends and develop skills relevant to their career growth.</p>
<p>LinkedIn Learning’s courses are typically created and taught by industry experts and available in several languages, making them accessible to a global audience.</p>
<p>Class Central’s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@suparn" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@suparn</a> searched LinkedIn Learning’s catalog and identified those that can be accessed without setting up a subscription. Many offer a free certificate.</p>
<p>He found <b>17</b> learning paths offering free certificates, and more than 400 individual courses with free certificates, for a total of about <b>460</b> hours of free online learning. Please note, we’re not sure how long these courses will continue to offer free certificates. Courses seem to periodically swap from paid to free and back again.</p>
<p>Below, you can find a selection. Visit our dedicated article for how to join LinkedIn free certificate courses and the full free certificate list: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/linkedin-learning-free-learning-paths/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">460+ Hours of Free LinkedIn Learning Certifications</a>.</p>

<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-career-essentials-in-generative-ai-by-microsoft-and-linkedin-301988" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Career Essentials in Generative AI by Microsoft and LinkedIn</a> (4-5 hours/6 items)</li>

<h2 id="meta"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free Meta Courses, Certificates, and Badges</span></h2>
<figure id="attachment_88627" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88627" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/meta.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-88627 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/meta.png" alt="" width="1024" height="722" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/meta.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/meta-300x212.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/meta-768x542.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88627" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/author/manoel/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Manoel&#8217;s</a> free <a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/activity/415305-get-started-with-ads-manager" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Meta Marketing certificate</a></figcaption></figure>
<p>Meta, widely recognized for its social media platforms Facebook and Instagram, has extended its influence into the realm of online education.</p>
<p>Meta has developed the <a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/catalog" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Meta Blueprint platform</a>, offering free mini-courses to prepare for <a href="https://certifications.facebookblueprint.com/student/catalog" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Meta’s certifications</a>. These courses help individuals leverage Meta’s platforms for marketing, advertising, and engagement. You can also find plenty of free offerings via YouTube.</p>
<p>Here’s a selection of popular offerings from Meta:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/activity/415305-get-started-with-ads-manager" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Get started with Ads Manager</a> from <i>Meta</i> via <i>Blueprint</i></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/path/211556-using-instagram-for-business" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Build an online business presence with Instagram</a> from <i>Meta</i> via <i>Blueprint</i></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/path/185998-promote-your-business-from-your-facebook-page" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Promote Your Business From Your Facebook Page</a> from <i>Meta</i> via <i>Blueprint</i></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.facebookblueprint.com/student/path/253135-meta-advantage-automation?sid_i=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Optimize your campaign with Meta Advantage</a> from <i>Meta</i> via <i>Blueprint</i></li>

<h2 id="gitlab"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free GitLab Courses &amp; Transcript</span></h2>
<figure id="attachment_88630" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88630" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/gitlab.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="wp-image-88630 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/gitlab.png" alt="" width="1024" height="544" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/gitlab.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/gitlab-300x159.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/gitlab-768x408.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88630" class="wp-caption-text">Some of the free courses available on GitLab LevelUp</figcaption></figure>
<p>GitLab, much like GitHub, offers developers a place to centralize and manage their code. To help developers use their platform, the GitLab team offers a range of free online courses through their LevelUp learning platform.</p>
<p><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/catalog" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab University</a> hosts around 90 free online courses. These include “micro-courses” and videos as well as a comprehensive learning path. The micro-courses are good for those seeking quick, focused insights into specific features of GitLab. They don’t include badges or certificates, but since the platform allows users to download a transcript of the courses they’ve completed, you may still demonstrate your learning. Certification exams are not free.</p>
<p>On the other hand, the comprehensive learning path offered on LevelUp does include a free certificate. It encompasses a broad overview of GitLab’s capabilities and best practices, in particular regarding CI.</p>
<p>Here are some courses offered by GitLab University:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/adding-pipeline-complexity" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Adding Pipeline Complexity</a></li>

<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/getting-started-with-cicd" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Getting Started with CI/CD</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-agile-project-management-s2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Agile Project Management</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-flow" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Flow</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-jira-integration" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Jira Integration</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-package-and-release-functions" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Package and Release Functions</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-runners" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Runners</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-technical-writing-fundamentals" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab Technical Writing Fundamentals</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/gitlab-with-git-essentials-s2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">GitLab with Git Essentials</a></li>

<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/introduction-to-registries" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Registries</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/introduction-to-security-scanning" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Security Scanning</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/migrating-from-circleci-to-gitlab" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Migrating from CircleCI to GitLab</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://university.gitlab.com/courses/migrating-from-gitlab-to-gitlab" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Migrating from GitLab to GitLab</a></li>

<h2 id="mongodb"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Free MongoDB Courses &amp; Transcript</span></h2>
<figure id="attachment_88631" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-88631" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/mongodb.png" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-full wp-image-88631" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/mongodb.png" alt="" width="1024" height="576" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/mongodb.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/mongodb-300x169.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/mongodb-768x432.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-88631" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/author/manoel/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Manoel&#8217;s</a> course dashboard on MongoDB University</figcaption></figure>
<p>MongoDB, known for its popular NoSQL database, offers free online courses on the MongoDB University. As you can imagine, this platform is dedicated to educating learners on all aspects of MongoDB.</p>
<p><a href="https://learn.mongodb.com/catalog?labels=%5B%22Free%2FPaid%22%5D&amp;values=%5B%22Free%22%5D" target="_blank" rel="noopener">MongoDB University</a> hosts 140+ offerings, which range in duration from simple units to comprehensive learning paths. The platform is a good resource for developers, database administrators, and anyone interested in mastering MongoDB.</p>
<p>While MongoDB University does not offer free certificates or badges, the platform allows learners to download a transcript of their completed courses, for those who want to showcase their MongoDB proficiency.</p>
<p>Here are some free courses offered on MongoDB University:</p>
<ul>

<p>Software reverse engineering (SRE) is the practice of analyzing a software system to extract design patterns and implementation information. This involves studying the program&#8217;s code (usually a low-level <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-assembly-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">assembly</a> or bytecode) to understand its behavior and functions.</p>

<h2 id="whatis">What is (Software) Reverse Engineering?</h2>
<p>Reverse engineering is the process of taking an object apart and understanding its design and functionality to understand how it works and potentially recreate it or create something similar. This technique has been used throughout history to understand the technology (especially military) of others, from the <a href="https://historylist.wordpress.com/2008/05/06/reverse-engineering-for-war" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ancient Egyptians capturing and incorporating fearsome Assyrian chariots into their own army</a>, to more recent examples when <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupolev_Tu-4" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the Soviets reversed engineered American planes</a> and <a href="https://nationalinterest.org/blog/reboot/america-went-great-lengths-seize-soviet-technology-during-cold-war-167780" target="_blank" rel="noopener">vice versa</a>.</p>
<p>In the information age, a new form of reverse engineering has emerged: Software Reverse Engineering (SRE). Instead of physical technology, digital technology can be taken apart and analyzed for information. This involves studying the program&#8217;s code and internal operations to understand its behavior and functions. Often, only the compiled machine code or bytecode is available, making it a challenge to translate low-level abstractions back into higher-level concepts.</p>
<p>SRE is a valuable tool for malware analysts and security researchers. They can use it to create patches and fix bugs in existing software. Analysts can even turn the tool against hackers and find vulnerabilities in malware.</p>
<p>If you&#8217;re interested in working in the cybersecurity field, or if you&#8217;re curious about how some piece of software works under the hood (but don’t violate any licensing agreements), learning SRE can be a useful skill to have.</p>

<h2 id="hackaday"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-reverse-engineering-with-ghidra-119213" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Free Ghidra Course for Beginners (Hackaday)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-reverse-engineering-with-ghidra-119213" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92385 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-hackaday.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-hackaday.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-hackaday-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-hackaday-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-reverse-engineering-with-ghidra-119213" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Reverse Engineering with Ghidra</a> on Hackaday is a <b>free</b> course that will teach you how to reverse engineer software using Ghidra, a free software reverse engineering tool developed by the NSA.</p>
<p>By the end of the course, you’ll have a good understanding of x86_64 architecture for Linux and be able to use different methodologies and approaches when reverse engineering an unknown program.</p>
<p>To take this course, you’ll need experience with <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-free-c-programming-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">C programming</a> and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-assembly-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Assembly</a> language.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand how software is built and compiled, from high-level languages to machine code</li>
<li aria-level="1">Use Ghidra to disassemble compiled bytecode and reconstruct x86 assembly-level instructions</li>
<li aria-level="1">Translate common C constructs (control flow, loops, variables, functions, etc.) into assembly code</li>
<li aria-level="1">Compare various reverse engineering tools and their pros/cons</li>
<li aria-level="1">Patch binaries to modify compiled program behavior</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore OS concepts such as system calls</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master advanced features: loading external libraries, performing patch analysis and diffing, generating checksums.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="malwareunicorn"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-101-66502" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Free Text Based Course With Hands-on Labs With Trusted Industry Leader (Malware Unicorn)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-101-66502" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92387 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-malwareunicorn.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-malwareunicorn.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-malwareunicorn-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-malwareunicorn-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-101-66502" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Reverse Engineering 101</a> hosted by Malware Unicorn is a <b>free</b> hands-on workshop that will teach you the fundamentals of reverse engineering x86 Windows malware. You&#8217;ll set up your own malware analysis environment and learn about operating systems and assembly concepts. You&#8217;ll also get to analyze malware hands-on using triage, static, and dynamic analysis.</p>
<p>To take this course, you’ll need at least 8 GB of RAM, 40 GB of storage, and an internet connection.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Set up a safe malware analysis environment using VirtualBox</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand key operating system and assembly concepts</li>
<li aria-level="1">Study the anatomy of a typical Portable Executable Windows Program</li>
<li aria-level="1">Dissect C-compiled assembly code</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore various types of malware and their attack flows</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn how malware infiltrates and hides in systems</li>
<li aria-level="1">Use popular Reverse Engineering tools like disassemblers and debuggers</li>
<li aria-level="1">Perform hands-on malware analysis using common methodologies:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Gather initial information about malware origins</li>
<li aria-level="2">Conduct triage analysis to identify malware characteristics</li>
<li aria-level="2">Execute static analysis to examine code without running the malware</li>
<li aria-level="2">Perform dynamic analysis to understand hidden functionality and behavior.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="tryhackme"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/tryhackme-windows-reversing-intro-119214" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Free Text and Exercise Based Intro to Windows SRE Using IDA (TryHackMe)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/tryhackme-windows-reversing-intro-119214" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92388 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-tryhackme.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-tryhackme.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-tryhackme-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-tryhackme-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>This <b>free</b> hands-on course introduces students to reverse engineering software on Windows. You’ll cover high-level concepts at a lower level and also be introduced to IDA, a popular reverse engineering tool, through the virtual machine provided (or on your own machine, if you’d like).</p>
<p>By the end of the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/tryhackme-windows-reversing-intro-119214" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Windows Reversing Intro</a> lab on TryHackMe, you’ll be able to perform more advanced reverse engineering techniques.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Master key IDA functionalities:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Disassembling</li>
<li aria-level="2">Decompiling</li>
<li aria-level="2">Debugging</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand functions and their stack frames:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Analyze how functions and loops appear in assembly language</li>
<li aria-level="2">Exploit frame pushing and popping to modify programs</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Identify common data structures in assembly code:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Stacks</li>
<li aria-level="2">Arrays</li>
<li aria-level="2">Classes (in object-oriented Windows environment)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Unmangle garbled C++ function names when reading DLLs.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="kevin"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-for-everyone-119218" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Free Gitbook Collection Of Text Based Courses on X86, Arm32, X64, Arm64 SRE (Kevin Thomas)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-for-everyone-119218" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92384 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-thomas.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-thomas.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-thomas-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-thomas-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-reverse-engineering-for-everyone-119218" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Reverse Engineering For Everyone!</a> is a <b>free</b> comprehensive reverse engineering tutorial covering x86, x64, 32-bit ARM &amp; 64-bit ARM architectures. Yes, all of them!</p>
<p>These tutorials will carry you from nothing up to the mid-basics of reverse engineering.</p>
<p>No prior knowledge of reverse engineering is needed to take this course.</p>
<p>In this course, you will learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">x86 and x64 architectures tutorials:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">You’ll learn about processor architectures, including registers and memory management. You’ll also learn assembly language and take a careful look at stacks and heaps. With this knowledge, you’ll be equipped with reversing engineering knowledge to identify malware with static and dynamic analysis, and then debug and reverse engineer them</li>
<li aria-level="2">Specifically for the x64 course, you’ll learn how the boot sector works and how it can be exploited, as well as look at various C programs translated into assembly code</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">32-bit and 64-bit ARM architectures tutorials:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">You’ll learn the ARM-32 bit architecture. You’ll take a look at the Von Neumann architecture, the instruction pipeline, as well as the registers involved. You’ll also write very basic C++ programs and then reverse them one at a time into ARM instructions. Then, you’ll learn how to debug and override these instructions.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Here is <a href="https://github.com/mytechnotalent/Reverse-Engineering" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the GitHub repository of the course</a> and the <a href="https://discord.com/invite/TC9V9RCr5U" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Discord server</a> to meet other reverse engineers.</p>

<h2 id="cybrary"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cybrary-malware-analysis-99277" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Reverse Engineering Malware Course (Cybrary)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cybrary-malware-analysis-99277" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92381 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-cybrary.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-cybrary.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-cybrary-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-cybrary-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cybrary-malware-analysis-99277" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Intro to Malware Analysis and Reverse Engineering</a> on Cybrary will give you the knowledge and skills needed to combat malware targeted towards organizations. It is designed for beginners in information technology to help prepare for the Certified Ethical Hacker (CEH) exam.</p>
<p>You’ll analyze and understand common malware tactics using reverse engineering, and then learn how to identify, isolate, and defend against these threats using malware analysis and reverse engineering tools.</p>
<p>No prior experience with programming or knowledge of assembly is required to take this course with <b>free limited access</b>. But, it is recommended that you have a general understanding of Networking, Operating System Internals, Programming, and Hacking.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand the limitations of antivirus software and the importance of malware analysis</li>
<li aria-level="1">Set up a malware analysis lab:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Configure a Windows XP Virtual Machine</li>
<li aria-level="2">Funnel traffic to a Kali Linux VM</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Perform dynamic analysis:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Identify different types of malware in real-time</li>
<li aria-level="2">Assess potential risks and impacts</li>
<li aria-level="2">Recognize indicators of compromise in a system</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Execute basic static analysis:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Analyze code and functionality without executing malware</li>
<li aria-level="2">Debug and disassemble malware samples</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement a hybrid approach combining dynamic and static analysis</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand and deal with packers:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Learn how malware uses compression and encryption to evade detection</li>
<li aria-level="2">Identify malware disguised as legitimate software</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master advanced techniques to bypass malware defenses:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Counter anti-VM measures</li>
<li aria-level="2">Overcome anti-disassembly tactics</li>
<li aria-level="2">Bypass other advanced malware protection mechanisms.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-reverse-engineering-security-hackers--119217" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92382 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-jared.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-jared.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-jared-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-jared-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-reverse-engineering-security-hackers--119217" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Security for Hackers and Developers: Reverse Engineering</a> is another course on Pluralsight that teaches you how to reverse engineer programs (including malware) through hands-on demos with IDA and Binary Ninja, both popular tools among reverse engineers. By the end of the <b>paid</b> course with <b>free trial</b>, you’ll know how to reverse engineer C and C++ programs with confidence.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Set up and master IDA Pro:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Understand its key functions</li>
<li aria-level="2">Use IDA Pro to find hidden passwords in applications</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Comprehend x86 assembly code:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Study the lowest level of code abstraction</li>
<li aria-level="2">Learn assembly calling conventions</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Analyze compiled programs:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Examine assembly code generated from C and C++ programs</li>
<li aria-level="2">Compare high-level C code with its corresponding assembly</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Perform binary patching:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Fix security vulnerabilities in compiled programs</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Customize IDA Pro:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Write scripts to enhance efficiency and productivity.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pentesteracademy-reverse-engineering-linux-32-bit-applications-119216" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92383 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-pentester.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-pentester.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-pentester-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/bcg-sre-pentester-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>

<p>By the end of this <b>paid</b> course, you’ll become familiar with how Linux applications work and their common flaws, how to locate these flaws manually or automatically with common reversing tools such as debuggers, fuzzers, Python scripts, and other scripting tools.</p>
<p>What You&#8217;ll Learn:</p>

<li aria-level="2">Learn basics of assembly language</li>
<li aria-level="2">Study Linux calling conventions</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Identify and exploit common security flaws:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Stack overflows</li>
<li aria-level="2">Heap overflows</li>
<li aria-level="2">Section overflows</li>
<li aria-level="2">First string flaws</li>
<li aria-level="2">Kernel flaws</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Automate reverse engineering tasks:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Utilize Python and shell scripting for increased productivity</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore advanced concepts:
<ul>
<li aria-level="2">Shellcoding techniques</li>
<li aria-level="2">Using Metasploit for exploit modules.</li>
</ul>

<p>I built this article following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">250K online courses</a> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/reverse-engineering" target="_blank" rel="noopener">900+ Reverse Engineering</a> courses by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener">learner</a>.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable, engaging content and fit in a set of criteria: comprehensive curriculum, affordability, release date, ratings and enrollments.</li>
</ol>

<h2 id="whatis">What is Programming?</h2>
<p>In essence, programming is the art of effectively telling a computer what to do. It is writing instructions for a computer to execute in order to accomplish a specific task. The simplest of things must be spelled out for the computer. Thanks to some clever mathematics and engineering, humans were able to make chips of sand understand the laws of logic.</p>
<p>Unfortunately, computers only understand the language of 0s and 1s, so us humans must communicate with them in a different way. People have invented many different languages that allow us to talk to the computer to get a result. These human-readable languages can be converted into the 0s and 1s that computers understand.</p>
<p>But different programmers try to achieve different tasks with computers. Some programmers want the computer to build websites (web developers), while others want to create useful tools (software engineers) or develop fun interactive media (game developers).</p>
<p>Since programming is so wide and diverse, there are many different industries and fields that one can specialize in, and some fields may pay more than others. Nonetheless, programmers are widely sought after as they keep the digital blood flowing.</p>
<p>According to the US Bureau of Labor Statistics, software development employment is expected to <a href="https://www.bls.gov/ooh/computer-and-information-technology/software-developers.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener">rise by 17%</a> through 2033. And according to <a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/programmer-salary-SRCH_KO0,10.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Glassdoor</a>, the national average salary for a programmer is $106K in the United States.</p>
<h2 id="trust">Why You Should Trust Us</h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a>, a Tripadvisor for online education, has helped 100 million learners find their next course. We’ve been combing through online education for more than a decade to aggregate a catalog of 250,000 online courses and 250,000 reviews written by our users. And we’re online learners ourselves: combined, the Class Central team has completed over 400 online courses, including online degrees.</p>

</ul>
<h2 id="michigan"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-4319" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Programming Course for Beginners (Michigan)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-4319" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92371 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-michigan.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-michigan.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-michigan-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-michigan-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>The first course I recommend to anyone new to programming is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-4319" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Programming for Everybody</a>, offered by the University of Michigan on Coursera. With over 3 million enrollments on Coursera, this <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free-to-audit</a> course is the most popular Python course out there and one of the most popular online courses ever.</p>
<p>The course introduces you to the Python programming language. Python is easy to learn due to its elegant simplicity. It is the most popular language according to <a href="https://www.tiobe.com/tiobe-index/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the TIOBE index</a>, and is incredibly versatile — capable of handling with ease tasks ranging from web development to machine learning.</p>
<p>This course is designed for complete beginners. It will teach you the foundations of programming which will transfer over to many other programming languages. All you need to know prior to taking this course is some basic arithmetic.</p>
<p>This course has been featured in the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/most-popular-online-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">most popular courses of all time</a> and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/collection/top-free-online-courses" target="_blank" rel="noopener">best courses of all time</a>.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand fundamental computing concepts and program execution</li>
<li aria-level="1">Install Python and choose a code editor (<a href="https://atom.io/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Atom</a> recommended)</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master basic Python syntax, including &#8220;Hello World&#8221; program</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn variables, expressions, and value storage/computation</li>
<li aria-level="1">Control program flow with conditionals (if/else) and loops (while/for)</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement functions and pass arguments for code reuse</li>
<li aria-level="1">Develop programs that accept user input, compute results, and provide output</li>
<li aria-level="1">Grasp the two core programming skills: language proficiency and logical &#8220;storytelling&#8221;.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="georgia"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-computing-in-python-i-fundamentals-and-procedural-programming-11469" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Rigorous and Well-Rounded Python Course for the Dedicated (Georgia Tech)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-computing-in-python-i-fundamentals-and-procedural-programming-11469" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92370 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-georgia.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-georgia.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-georgia-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-georgia-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-computing-in-python-i-fundamentals-and-procedural-programming-11469" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computing in Python I: Fundamentals and Procedural Programming</a> is a <b>free to audit</b> course by the Georgia Institute of Technology on edX.</p>
<p>Although the course uses Python as the instructional programming language, it also exposes you to several fundamental concepts in programming and computer science. Concepts that carry over to every other programming language out there. By the end of this course, you’ll understand how to write programs that carry out complex mathematical operations, like calculating the interest rate necessary to reach a savings goal.</p>
<p>The course is taught by Dr. David Joyner. My colleague, Manoel, has taken four of his courses in his <a href="https://omscs.gatech.edu/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online master’s degree</a> (and he has even met the guy!). He has only good things to say about David Joyner and his courses, which are always carefully thought out, in particular in terms of instructional design and teaching methods.</p>
<p>The only thing you need prior to taking this course is basic arithmetic.</p>
<p>The course also comes with an online book. Each week is dedicated to a specific area of computer science and programming, so you may skip to areas you already know to make the best use of your time.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand computer basics and code processing</li>
<li aria-level="1">Set up a programming environment</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master the write-run-debug cycle and code analysis</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn procedural programming in Python</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore variables, data types, and operators</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement complex mathematical operations in code</li>
<li aria-level="1">Grasp fundamental programming concepts applicable to all languages.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="washington"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-languages-452" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Excellent Intermediate Functional Programming Course (Washington)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-languages-452" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92376 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-washington.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-washington.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-washington-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-washington-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>Why functional programming? Well, functional programming encourages you to write robust, reusable, composable, and elegant programs. Indeed, many of the most important ideas in modern languages have their roots in functional programming. Get ready to learn a fresh and beautiful way to look at software and how to have fun building it.</p>
<p>Offered by the University of Washington on Coursera, this free-to-audit course introduces you to the basic concepts of programming languages, with a focus on functional programming.</p>
<p>The course is designed to teach students the core ideas around which every programming language is built upon. It aims to show you the fundamental concepts that can be found and expressed in almost all programming languages, using these three different languages as an example. This allows you to think more deeply about the underlying ideas, and about how these ideas fit together instead of being distracted by surface-level syntax.</p>
<p>This course is one of the most challenging MOOCs out there, but it is immensely rewarding. Not only will you learn new languages faster, but you will also become a better programmer even in languages you don’t use!</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-languages-452" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Programming Languages, Part A</a> assumes you have some programming background or have taken one or two introductory programming courses. If you’re a complete beginner, you should check out the other courses on this guide before tackling this course.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Master SML basics: variables, functions, conditionals, and data structures</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore recursion, pattern-matching, and tail recursion</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand compound data types and user-defined types</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn about first-class functions, closures, and lexical scope</li>
<li aria-level="1">Study type inference and polymorphic types</li>
<li aria-level="1">Grasp SML&#8217;s module system for encapsulation and abstraction</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore function equivalence in functional programming</li>
<li aria-level="1">Set up and use <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/emacs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Emacs</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_ML_of_New_Jersey" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SML/NJ</a> development environment.</li>
</ul>
<p>Note that, Part A is the first of the <i>Programming Languages</i> series, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-languages-part-b-6920" target="_blank" rel="noopener">followed by Part B</a> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-languages-part-c-7187" target="_blank" rel="noopener">and Part C</a>. You are recommended to complete the entire series to fully experience the elegance of functional programming.</p>

<h2 id="princeton"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs-programming-java-13151" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Awesome All-Around Introduction to Java Programming (Princeton)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs-programming-java-13151" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92372 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-princeton.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-princeton.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-princeton-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-princeton-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs-programming-java-13151" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computer Science: Programming with a Purpose</a> by Princeton University on Coursera is a comprehensive introduction to programming in Java.</p>
<p>The intent of this course is to teach programming in a scientific context. It teaches basic skills for computational problem solving applicable in many modern computing environments. After taking this course not only will you be proficient in Java, but you will also understand several fundamental concepts found in other programming languages.</p>
<p>This course is suitable for first-year college students and even motivated high schoolers. It doesn’t require prior programming experience.</p>
<p>What You&#8217;ll Learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand the purpose and historical context of programming</li>
<li aria-level="1">Develop your first Java program and learn basic programming concepts</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master conditional statements, loops, and arrays</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement input/output operations for user interaction</li>
<li aria-level="1">Create fractal drawings and animations using Java</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore modular programming with functions and libraries</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn recursion through classic examples like the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tower_of_Hanoi" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tower of Hanoi</a></li>
<li aria-level="1">Analyze program performance and running time</li>
<li aria-level="1">Dive into object-oriented programming and create custom data types</li>
<li aria-level="1">Apply complex numbers to visualize the Mandelbrot set</li>
<li aria-level="1">Compare different programming languages and paradigms</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore advanced concepts like garbage collection, type checking, and functional programming.</li>
</ul>
<p>Note that, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs-programming-java-13151" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computer Science: Programming with a Purpose</a> covers the first half of the book <a href="https://www.informit.com/store/computer-science-an-interdisciplinary-approach-9780134076423" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computer Science: An Interdisciplinary Approach</a>. The other half is covered by the next course, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/computerscience2-10671" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Computer Science: Algorithms, Theory, and Machines</a>.</p>

<h2 id="rice"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interactivepython1-408" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Project-Based Course for Hands-On Learners (Rice)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interactivepython1-408" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92373 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-rice.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-rice.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-rice-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-rice-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"> </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interactivepython1-408" target="_blank" rel="noopener">An Introduction to Interactive Programming in Python (Part 1)</a> by Rice University on Coursera aims to help students with very little to no programming background learn the basics of building simple interactive applications in Python. It is heavily project-based, encouraging you to build and research things from scratch, an invaluable skill for developers in the real world.</p>
<p>While it’s a beginner course, it isn’t meant to be easy. The philosophy of the instructors is that the harder you work, the faster you learn. So, you’ll have to dedicate a significant amount of effort to complete the course.</p>
<p>As a prerequisite, you’ll only need some background in high school mathematics (like the Pythagorean theorem). This course uses Python 2 (older version) but is nonetheless still a good introduction to programming.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Basic Python arithmetic and variable assignment</li>
<li aria-level="1">Function implementation and debugging techniques</li>
<li aria-level="1">Logical operators and conditional statements</li>
<li aria-level="1">Event-driven programming and GUI creation</li>
<li aria-level="1">String processing and canvas drawing</li>
<li aria-level="1">List manipulation and keyboard input handling</li>
<li aria-level="1">Game development, including a Pong clone</li>
<li aria-level="1">Local vs. global variables</li>
<li aria-level="1">Simple animation and game state tracking.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="duke"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-fundamentals-9574" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Programming — Algorithm Focused (Duke)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-fundamentals-9574" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92367 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-duke.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-duke.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-duke-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-duke-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;"> </span>Programming is fundamentally about figuring out how to solve various classes of problems and write algorithms, a clear set of steps to solve any problem in its class.</p>
<p>Duke University’s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/programming-fundamentals-9574" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Programming Fundamentals</a> will introduce you to a powerful problem-solving process — the Seven Steps — which you can use to solve any programming problem. In this course, you will learn how to develop an algorithm, then move on to reading and understanding code, as well as comprehending how programming concepts relate to algorithms.</p>
<p>This free-to-audit course uses the C programming language. You don’t need any programming experience to take this course.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Master the Seven Steps process for solving programming problems</li>
<li aria-level="1">Develop and formulate precise algorithms</li>
<li aria-level="1">Read and understand code with various programming constructs</li>
<li aria-level="1">Execute code by hand to track program state</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore different data types and their binary representations</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand type-related programming concepts and avoid common mistakes</li>
<li aria-level="1">Develop and test a custom sorting algorithm.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="vanderbilt"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/matlab-3396" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introductory Programming Course for Engineers and Scientists with MATLAB (Vanderbilt)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/matlab-3396" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92375 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-vanderbilt.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-vanderbilt.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-vanderbilt-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-vanderbilt-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>Are you an engineer or a scientist with little to no coding experience who wants to learn programming to boost your marketable skills? <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/matlab-3396" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Programming with MATLAB</a> is the perfect course for you.</p>
<p>You’ve most likely heard of MATLAB before, as it is heavily used in industry and academia, from the natural sciences, through all disciplines of engineering, finance and beyond. This is because MATLAB is easy to learn, versatile and very useful for scientific computing. The design of the language makes it possible to write powerful programs that solve complex tasks in just a few lines, compared to other programming languages like C++ or Java.</p>
<p>Hence, a solid background in MATLAB is an excellent skill if you’re interested in scientific computing.</p>
<p>Nevertheless, this course is not a MATLAB tutorial. It is an introductory programming course that uses MATLAB to illustrate general concepts in computer science and programming. Upon completion, you’ll understand the general concepts of computer science and programming, and gain a solid foundation in the use of MATLAB.</p>
<p>Students taking the course will get a MATLAB Online license free of charge for the duration of the course.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Navigate MATLAB environment and user interface</li>
<li aria-level="1">Use MATLAB as an advanced calculator and create plots</li>
<li aria-level="1">Work with matrices: define, manipulate, and perform operations</li>
<li aria-level="1">Create and use functions for modular programming</li>
<li aria-level="1">Utilize MATLAB&#8217;s built-in functions and debugging tools</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement basic programming constructs: if-statements, for-loops, while-loops</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore MATLAB&#8217;s 15 fundamental data types, including numbers and strings</li>
<li aria-level="1">Handle file I/O operations with various file formats</li>
<li aria-level="1">Navigate folders using MATLAB commands.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="fcc"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/freecodecamp-responsive-web-design-34059" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Responsive Web Design Course for Newbies (freeCodeCamp)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/freecodecamp-responsive-web-design-34059" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92369 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-freecodecamp.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-freecodecamp.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-freecodecamp-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-freecodecamp-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>If you’re a complete newbie with no programming experience who wants to learn how to build websites, you should start with this course.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/freecodecamp-responsive-web-design-34059" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Responsive Web Design</a> teaches you the languages that developers use to build webpages: HTML (Hypertext Markup Language) for content, and CSS (Cascading Style Sheets) for design. The course with <b>free certificate</b> guides you through the basics of HTML and CSS by building many different bite-sized projects and a 5 big ones!</p>
<p>What You&#8217;ll Learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">HTML basics: structure, tags, and forms</li>
<li aria-level="1">CSS fundamentals: colors, fonts, and box model</li>
<li aria-level="1">Responsive design using CSS flexbox and grid</li>
<li aria-level="1">Web accessibility and typography</li>
<li aria-level="1">CSS advanced techniques: pseudo-selectors, variables, and animations</li>
<li aria-level="1">Building interactive elements and animations.</li>
</ul>
<p>Projects:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://codepen.io/freeCodeCamp/full/VPaoNP" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Survey form</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://codepen.io/freeCodeCamp/full/zNqgVx" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tribute page</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://codepen.io/freeCodeCamp/full/NdrKKL" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Technical documentation page</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://codepen.io/freeCodeCamp/full/RKRbwL" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Product landing page</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://codepen.io/freeCodeCamp/full/zNBOYG" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Personal portfolio webpage</a></li>
</ol>

<h2 id="ucdavis"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/javascript-basics-36577" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best JavaScript Course for Beginners (UC Davis)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/javascript-basics-36577" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92374 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-ucdavis.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-ucdavis.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-ucdavis-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-ucdavis-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>If you have done the previous course, or you have tried building a nice-looking website with HTML/CSS but don’t know where to go from there, pick this course from the University of California, Davis.</p>
<p>JavaScript is the programming language used by over 97% of websites. It is used to manipulate the HTML and CSS of a webpage, after it has loaded from the server. In a way, it brings life to a static HTML/CSS website.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/javascript-basics-36577" target="_blank" rel="noopener">JavaScript Basics</a> — well, introduces you to the basics of JavaScript. You’ll learn the reason JavaScript was developed in the first place, and how this impacts the way JavaScript is currently written and in future releases. By the end of the course, you’ll have the necessary skills needed to build a simple vacation destination list web application.</p>
<p>You’ll need some background in HTML and CSS to take this course. Other than that, no programming experience is required.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">JavaScript basics: syntax, variables, and arrays</li>
<li aria-level="1">Control structures: sequence, selection, and loops</li>
<li aria-level="1">Function creation and implementation</li>
<li aria-level="1">DOM manipulation and event handling</li>
<li aria-level="1">Variable scoping and best practices</li>
<li aria-level="1">Building interactive web elements (e.g., slideshows).</li>
</ul>
<p>Projects:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Simple slideshow</li>
<li aria-level="1">Vacation destination list application</li>
<li aria-level="1">Advanced distance converter.</li>
</ul>
<p>Key skills developed:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Writing and troubleshooting JavaScript code</li>
<li aria-level="1">Creating interactive websites</li>
<li aria-level="1">Manipulating webpage content dynamically</li>
<li aria-level="1">Designing and building basic web applications.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="edinburgh"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/codeyourself-2938" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Friendliest Scratch Programming Course for Beginners (Edinburgh)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/codeyourself-2938" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92379 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-edinburgh-2.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-edinburgh-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-edinburgh-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/bcg-programming-edinburgh-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>If you have looked through all the courses in this list and felt intimidated by their difficulty and strangeness, this last course is for you.</p>
<p>A collaboration between the University of Edinburgh and Universidad ORT Uruguay, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/codeyourself-2938" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Code Yourself! An Introduction to Programming</a> will teach you how to program in Scratch. More importantly, it will introduce you to the fundamental principles of computing, helping you think like a software engineer.</p>
<p>Scratch is an easy-to-use drag-and-drop visual programming language. It is an educational tool for programming, so many of the programming concepts in other languages are represented easily here.</p>
<p>What You&#8217;ll Learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Basic programming concepts: algorithms, sequences, and loops</li>
<li aria-level="1">Control structures: if-then statements, if-then-else selections</li>
<li aria-level="1">Variables and complex conditions</li>
<li aria-level="1">Events, visual and sound effects in Scratch</li>
<li aria-level="1">Computational thinking: abstraction and decomposition</li>
<li aria-level="1">Software engineering practices: testing and documentation</li>
<li aria-level="1">Procedures, cloning, and code reusability</li>
<li aria-level="1">Software development approaches and game creation.</li>
</ul>
