<h2 id="tested">How We Made Our Picks and Tested Them</h2>
<p>I built this guide following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in my previous BCGs. It involves a three-step process:</p>
<p><b>First</b>, let me introduce myself. I’m a content writer for <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a>, the leading search engine for online courses.</p>
<p>I (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@elham</a>) built this article in collaboration with my friend and colleague<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@manoel" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> @manoel</a>.</p>
<p>To build this guide, we scoured through Class Central’s database of close to 60K online courses for the best courses by looking at things like ratings, reviews, and bookmarks. This data-driven process helped us come up with a bunch of the best courses out there.</p>
<p>Good courses get noticed by word of mouth — and the very best tend to gather a lot of attention. That said, reviews don’t always tell the whole story. In fact, some courses are so good at hugging the spotlight that other excellent resources can go unnoticed. So the next step was to bring our own knowledge of online education into the mix.</p>
<p><b>Second</b>, we used our experience as online learners to evaluate each preliminary pick.</p>
<p>We both come from computer science backgrounds and are prolific online learners, having completed about 45 MOOCs between us. Additionally, Manoel has an<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/open-university-insiders-perspective/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> online bachelor’s in computer science</a>, while I am currently completing my foundation in computer science. So programming is a subject that we were both very familiar with.</p>
<p>We analyzed and sifted through the courses, picking them one by one. We bounced ideas off each other and made iterative improvements to the guide, until we were both satisfied with the end result: the BCG you’re reading right now.</p>
<p><b>Third</b>, during our research, we came across courses that we felt were well-made but unfortunately weren’t well-known. If we adopted a purely data-centric approach, we would have to leave those courses out of the guide, if only because they had fewer enrollments.</p>
<p>Instead, we favored a holistic approach. To spice up this BCG, we’ve added a wide range of courses of various programming languages to hopefully appeal to our reader’s preference.</p>
<p>After going through this process — combining Class Central data, our experience as lifelong learners, and a lot of editing — we arrived at our final selection. So far, we’ve spent more than 10 hours building this article, and we intend to continue updating it in the future.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@fabio" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Fabio</i></a><i> revised the research and the latest version of this article.</i></p>

<h2 id="whatis">What is Applied AI &amp; ML?</h2>
<p>You may know a bit about AI and machine learning from here and there. Or perhaps, you’ve actually gotten quite good at them. It’s understandable. These fields are very promising. But now, you don’t really know what to do with the knowledge and skills you’ve learned.</p>
<p>(Just in case you actually don&#8217;t know these fields yet, AI is the field of computer science that focuses on allowing computers to demonstrate human-like intelligence. Machine learning is one branch of AI that deals with learning from large amounts of data. If you’re new to these fields, have a look at our <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-ai-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Artificial Intelligence</a> or <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-machine-learning-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Machine Learning</a> guides.)</p>
<p>The best way to cement your understanding of AI and ML is to put your knowledge into practice. And as it happens, there are countless, powerful ways to apply AI and machine learning. And by doing so, you can develop industry-relevant skills through projects that are not only useful, but fascinating.</p>
<h2 id="trust">Why You Should Trust Us</h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central</a>, a Tripadvisor for online education, has helped 100 million learners find their next course. We’ve been combing through online education for more than a decade to aggregate a catalog of 250,000 online courses and 250,000 reviews written by our users. And we’re online learners ourselves: combined, the Class Central team has completed over 400 online courses, including online degrees.</p>

<h2 id="convolutional"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/convolutional-neural-networks-9057" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Comprehensive Convolutional Neural Networks Course (DeepLearning.AI)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/convolutional-neural-networks-9057" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92357 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-convolutional.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-convolutional.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-convolutional-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-convolutional-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/convolutional-neural-networks-9057" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Convolutional Neural Networks</a> by DeepLearning.AI is a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free-to-audit</a> course that explores the world of computer vision and its applications. From autonomous driving to face recognition and radiology image analysis, you&#8217;ll learn to build and apply convolutional neural networks to various visual tasks.</p>
<p>Prerequisites: Intermediate Python skills, basic understanding of linear algebra and machine learning.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Master the fundamentals of Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) and their architecture</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement deep neural models for multi-class image classification</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore case studies of effective CNNs (LeNet-5, ResNet, Inception network)</li>
<li aria-level="1">Tackle object localization and detection using ConvNets and U-nets</li>
<li aria-level="1">Build a Siamese network for face recognition</li>
<li aria-level="1">Apply neural style transfer using deep ConvNets to generate art.</li>
</ul>

<p><a href="https://www.nobledesktop.com/certificates/data-science?utm_source=class-central&amp;utm_medium=referral" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-93620 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/bcg-applied-ai-ml-noble-desktop.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/bcg-applied-ai-ml-noble-desktop.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/bcg-applied-ai-ml-noble-desktop-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/bcg-applied-ai-ml-noble-desktop-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>

<h2 id="toronto"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/intro-self-driving-cars-13140" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Intro to Self-Driving Cars for Engineers (University of Toronto)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/intro-self-driving-cars-13140" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92363 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-toronto.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-toronto.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-toronto-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-toronto-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/intro-self-driving-cars-13140" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Self-Driving Cars</a> by the University of Toronto dives into the innovative world of autonomous vehicles. In this <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free-to-audit</a> course, you&#8217;ll explore terminology, design considerations, and safety assessments of self-driving cars.</p>
<p>Note: This advanced course requires a background in engineering or robotics with strong foundations in Linear Algebra, Statistics, Calculus, and Physics, plus Python 3 programming skills. You&#8217;ll need a somewhat recent 64-bit Windows or Ubuntu machine with 8 GB RAM to run the CARLA simulator.</p>
<p>What you’ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Explore the history and recent progress of autonomous vehicles</li>
<li aria-level="1">Break down the elements of driving, from identifying road signs to predicting actions</li>
<li aria-level="1">Examine various self-driving car hardware configurations and software stacks</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand environmental representation for decision-making in autonomous vehicles</li>
<li aria-level="1">Study safety considerations in autonomous vehicle design, both software and hardware</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn vehicle modeling and control, including localization, route following, and executing complex maneuvers</li>
<li aria-level="1">Test control designs and understand challenges of driving at vehicle performance limits</li>
<li aria-level="1">Develop control code for a self-driving car in a race track simulation (CARLA environment) as your final project.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="michigan"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-machine-learning-6673" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Applied Machine Learning Course in Python (University of Michigan)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-machine-learning-6673" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92361 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-michigan.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-michigan.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-michigan-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-michigan-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/python-machine-learning-6673" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Applied Machine Learning in Python</a> by the University of Michigan is a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-signup-for-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free-to-audit</a>, beginner-friendly course that teaches practical machine learning techniques and concepts. You&#8217;ll learn to differentiate between supervised and unsupervised learning, select specific features for model training, and implement machine learning analyses in Python.</p>
<p>Prerequisites: Python programming skills, familiarity with numpy, pandas, and matplotlib libraries.</p>
<p>Recommended (not required): <a href="https://www.oreilly.com/library/view/introduction-to-machine/9781449369880/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Machine Learning with Python</a> textbook.</p>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Understand fundamental machine learning concepts (supervised vs. unsupervised learning)</li>
<li aria-level="1">Implement k-nearest neighbors algorithm using scikit-learn</li>
<li aria-level="1">Explore supervised learning methods for classification and regression</li>
<li aria-level="1">Balance model complexity and generalization</li>
<li aria-level="1">Evaluate and select models using various performance metrics</li>
<li aria-level="1">Study advanced supervised learning methods: tree ensembles and neural networks</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn to avoid data leakage and biases in model training.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="georgia"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udacity-introduction-to-computer-vision-1022" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Best Intro to Computer Vision and Applications (Georgia Institute of Technology)</a></h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udacity-introduction-to-computer-vision-1022" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92358 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-georgia.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-georgia.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-georgia-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-georgia-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>Teaching a computer to see and interpret images is fascinating, but before showing computers what images are, we too must know how images work.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udacity-introduction-to-computer-vision-1022" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Computer Vision</a> by Georgia Institute of Technology offers a comprehensive exploration of image analysis and information extraction. This content-rich course covers fundamental concepts including feature detection, motion tracking, camera calibration, and image stabilization.</p>
<p>Prerequisites:</p>
<ul>

<li aria-level="1">Proficiency in MATLAB and/or Python with NumPy</li>
<li aria-level="1">Linear algebra and vector calculus</li>
<li aria-level="1">Experience with signal processing (helpful but not required).</li>
</ul>
<p>What you&#8217;ll learn:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Explore the relationship between computational models, algorithms, and real images in computer vision</li>
<li aria-level="1">Master image processing techniques for various computer vision applications</li>
<li aria-level="1">Understand camera geometry, models, and multiple view relationships</li>
<li aria-level="1">Learn feature detection and matching across images</li>
<li aria-level="1">Study light interaction with materials and image formation</li>
<li aria-level="1">Analyze motion in videos and implement object tracking</li>
<li aria-level="1">Introduce machine learning concepts for classification and recognition in computer vision.</li>
</ul>

<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/classification-vector-spaces-in-nlp-20321" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-92356 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-classification.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-classification.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-classification-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/bcg-applied-ai-ml-classification-768x384.png 768w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>

<li aria-level="1">Develop a machine translation algorithm (English to French).</li>

<li aria-level="1">Focus on practical MLOps implementation strategies</li>

<h2 id="tested">How We Made Our Picks and Tested Them</h2>
<p>I built this article following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous BCGs (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<p><b>First</b>, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@manoel" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@manoel</a> and I (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@elham</a>) started building this guide by leveraging Class Central’s database of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">250K+ online courses</a>. We took a look at things like ratings, reviews, and course bookmarks to make a preliminary selection.</p>
<p>This data-driven approach helped us sift through and pinpoint some of the best courses available out there. Most good courses don’t go unnoticed. The very best tend to gather a lot of attention and excellent reviews!</p>
<p>That said, ratings and reviews don’t always tell the whole story. Some courses may be outdated or archived. So the next step was to bring our personal knowledge of online education into the mix.</p>
<p><b>Second</b>, we used our experience as online learners to evaluate each of our initial picks. We bounced ideas off each other and made iterative improvements to the guide until we were both satisfied with the end result.</p>
<p>We both come from computer science backgrounds and are prolific online learners, having completed about 45 MOOCs between us. Additionally, Manoel has an online bachelor’s in computer science, and I am currently completing my foundation in computer science. Hence, AI and ML are topics we’re both familiar with.</p>
<p><b>Third</b>, during our research, we came across courses that felt well-made but weren’t all that popular. If we adopted a purely data-centric approach, we would have to leave those courses out of the article, if only because they had fewer enrollments and ratings.</p>
<p>Instead, we took a more holistic approach. We spiced up this list by including a wide variety of Applied AI &amp; ML courses to cater to a diverse range of learners.</p>
<p>After going through this process — combining Class Central data, our experience as lifelong learners, and lots of editing — we arrived at our final guide. So far, we’ve spent more than 10 hours building this BCG, and we intend to continue updating it in the future.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@fabio" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Fabio</i></a><i> revised the research and the latest version of this article.</i></p>
